### ๐ 6. ุงูุชูุงูู ุงูุชููู ุงููุชูุฏู (Advanced Tech Integration)

#### ๐พ ูุงุนุฏุฉ ุงูุจูุงูุงุช ุงููุญุณูุฉ:

**ุฌุฏูู ุงููุฑุถู (Patients):**
```sql
CREATE TABLE patients (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100),
    age INT,
    condition VARCHAR(50),
    priority ENUM('LOW', 'MEDIUM', 'HIGH', 'CRITICAL'),
    arrival_time TIMESTAMP,
    treatment_start TIMESTAMP,
    treatment_end TIMESTAMP,
    satisfaction_score INT(0-10),
    payment_method ENUM('CASH', 'INSURANCE', 'FREE'),
    total_cost DECIMAL(10,2),
    assigned_doctor_id INT,
    department_id INT,
    notes TEXT
);
```

**ุฌุฏูู ุงูููุธููู (Staff):**
```sql
CREATE TABLE staff (
    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(100),
    role ENUM('DOCTOR', 'NURSE', 'ADMIN', 'TECHNICIAN'),
    specialization VARCHAR(50),
    energy_level INT(0-100),
    morale_level INT(0-100),
    skill_level INT(1-10),
    salary DECIMAL(8,2),
    hire_date DATE,
    shift_type ENUM('DAY', 'NIGHT', 'WEEKEND'),
    vacation_days_remaining INT,
    performance_rating DECIMAL(3,2)
);
```

**ุฌุฏูู ุงูููุงู (Missions):**
```sql

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    title VARCHAR(200),
    description TEXT,
    requirements JSON,
    rewards JSON,
    difficulty ENUM('EASY', 'MEDIUM', 'HARD', 'EXPERT'),
    time_limit INT, -- ูู ุงูุฏูุงุฆู
    status ENUM('AVAILABLE', 'IN_PROGRESS', 'COMPLETED', 'FAILED'),
    completion_date TIMESTAMP
);
```

**ุฌุฏูู ุงูุฃููุงู (Finance):**
```sql

    id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    type ENUM('INCOME', 'EXPENSE'),
    category VARCHAR(50),
    amount DECIMAL(10,2),
    description TEXT,
    date TIMESTAMP,
    related_patient_id INT,
    related_staff_id INT,
    related_department_id INT
);
```
